>>> ../datae\audio\courses\{{Sadlier-Oxford Vocabulary Workshop}} ## us/definitions ## {links}
'{abase}' is a verb meaning 'to lower, degrade or humble'.ogg
'{abashed}' is an adjective and participle meaning 'embarrassed' or 'ashamed'.ogg
'{abate}' is a verb that has several meanings.ogg
'{abate}' is a verb that has several meanings.txt
'{abdicate}' is a verb meaning 'to resign' or 'to disown'.ogg
'{abduct}' is a verb meaning 'to kidnap' or 'to carry off by force'.ogg
'{abet}' is a verb meaning to encourage or assist especially in something wrong or unworthy.ogg
'{abhor}' is a verb meaning to regard with horror or to hate deeply.ogg
'{abjure}' is a verb meaning to avoid or repudiate.ogg
'{abnormal}' is an adjective meaning not usual or not typical.ogg
'{abominable}' is an adjective meaning arousing hatred or disgusting.ogg
'{abominate}' is a verb meaning to have an intense dislike or hatred for.ogg
'{abound}' is a verb meaning to be plentiful or to be filled.ogg
'{abridge}' is a verb meaning to make shorter.ogg
'{abscond}' is a verb meaning to run off and hide.ogg
'{absolve}' is a verb meaning to clean from blame, responsibility or guilt.ogg
'{abstain}' is a verb meaning to stay away from doing something by one's own choice.ogg
'{abstemious}' is an adjective meaning moderate or sparing, or characterized by abstinence and self-discipline.ogg
'{abut}' is a verb meaning to join at one end or to support.ogg
'{abyss}' is a noun meaning a deep or bottomless pit.ogg
'{accede}' is a verb that means either to yield to or to assume a dignity or office.ogg
'{accelerate}' is a verb meaning to speed up or to bring about more quickly.ogg
'{acclimate}' is a verb meaning to adapt to a new environment or situation.ogg
'{accommodate}' is a verb meaning to do a favor or service for.ogg
'{accommodate}' is a verb meaning to do a favor or service for.txt
'{accomplice}' is a noun meaning someone who takes part in a crime.ogg
'{accrue}' is a verb meaning to grow or accumulate in the course of time or to happen as a natural result.ogg
'{acculturation}' is a noun meaning the modification of social patterns, traits or structures.ogg
'{acculturation}' is a noun meaning the modification of social patterns, traits or structures.txt
'{acme}' is a noun meaning the highest point.ogg
'{acquiesce}' is a verb meaning to accept without protest or to submit.ogg
'{acquit}' is a verb meaning to declare not guilty or discharge completely or to conduct oneself.ogg
'{acrid}' is an adjective meaning harsh in taste or odour, or sharp in manner or temper.ogg
'{acrimonious}' is an adjective meaning stinging or bitter in temper or tone.ogg
'{actuate}' is a verb meaning to move to action or to impel.ogg
'{acute}' is an adjective with several meanings including.ogg
'{acute}' is an adjective with several meanings including.txt
'{ad infinitum}' is an adverb meaning endlessly.ogg
'{adage}' is a noun meaning a proverb or wise saying.ogg
'{adhere}' is a verb meaning to stick to or remain attach, or to be devoted as a follower or supporter.ogg
'{adjacent}' is an adjective meaning near, next to or adjoining.ogg
'{adjourn}' is a verb meaning to stop for a time or to move to another place.ogg
'{admonish}' is a verb meaning to caution, scold or remind.ogg
'{adroit}' is an adjective meaning skillful or expert.ogg
'{adulation}' is a noun meaning praise or flattery that is excessive.ogg
'{adulterate}' is a verb meaning to make worse by the addition of something of lesser value.ogg
'{adventitious}' is an adjective meaning resulting from chance, or accidental or not essential.ogg
'{advent}' is a noun meaning an arrival or coming into existence.ogg
'{adversary}' is a noun meaning an enemy or opponent.ogg
'{adverse}' is an adjective meaning unfavorable or working against or hostile.ogg
'{affable}' is an adjective meaning courteous or pleasant, sociable or easy to speak to.ogg
'{affiliated}' is an adjective and participle meaning associated or connected.ogg
'{affirm}' is a verb meaning to declare to be true, or to confirm.ogg
'{affliction}' is a noun meaning a physical ailment, a cause of pain or trouble, or a misfortune.ogg
'{affluence}' is a noun meaning wealth, riches or prosperity, or great abundance.ogg
'{agenda}' is a noun meaning the program for a meeting, or an outline or plan of things to be done or considered.ogg
'{aggrandize}' is a verb meaning to increase in greatness, power or wealth.ogg
'{aggrandize}' is a verb meaning to increase in greatness, power or wealth.txt
'{aghast}' is an adjective meaning filled with amazement, disgust, fear or terror.ogg
'{agitation}' is a noun meaning a violent movement, noisy confusion or excitement.ogg
'{ajar}' may be used as an adjective or adverb meaning hardly open.ogg
'{akin}' is an adjective meaning related by blood, or having similar characteristics or qualities.ogg
'{alacrity}' is a noun meaning cheerful readiness or eager action.ogg
'{alienate}' is a verb meaning to make hostile or to transfer.ogg
'{allegiance}' is a noun meaning the loyalty or obligation to a government, nation or cause.ogg
'{alleviate}' is a verb meaning to relieve or make more bearable.ogg
'{alliance}' is a noun meaning adjoining together for some common purpose.ogg
'{allocate}' is a verb meaning to set apart for a special purpose or to distribute.ogg
'{allot}' is a verb meaning to assign or distribute into shares.ogg
'{allude}' is a verb meaning to refer to casually or indirectly.ogg
'{aloof}' is an adjective meaning withdrawn or standing apart from others.ogg
'{altercation}' is a noun meaning an angry argument.ogg
'{amalgamate}' is a verb meaning to unite or to combine elements onto a unified whole.ogg
'{amass}' is a verb meaning to bring or come together.ogg
'{ambidextrous}' is an adjective meaning able to use both hands equally well, or deceitful and hypocritical.ogg
'{ameliorate}' is a verb meaning to improve or to correct a flaw or shortcoming.ogg
'{amenable}' is an adjective meaning willing to follow advice or authority, tractable, or submissive, or responsive.ogg
'{amicable}' is an adjective meaning peaceful or friendly.ogg
'{ample}' is an adjective meaning more than enough or large and spacious.ogg
'{animosity}' is a noun meaning strong dislike or bitter hostility.ogg
'{deem}' is a verb meaning 'to believe' or 'to have an opinion'.ogg
'{devastate}' is a verb meaning 'to destrory' or 'lay waste'.ogg
'{elusive}' is an adjective meaning 'difficult to catch or hold' or 'hard to explain or understand'.ogg
'{generate}' is a verb meaning 'to bring into existence' or 'to be the cause of'.ogg
'{ingratitude}' is a noun meaning 'a lack of thankfulness'.ogg
